Children can then select the letters that make up word with the ability to revisit the completed word as many times as necessary.\r\n\r\nIn practise mode, the completed word is not shown, but feedback is provided to indicate whether the word is spelt correctly with advancement to the next word only possible when the word has been correctly completed.\r\n\r\nIn check and test mode, no hints on the correct spelling of the word are provided and all letters of the alphabet are options to be selected.\r\n\r\nThis app is suitable for preschool children wanting to get a head start on spelling before starting school as well as older children who are already at school and who want to further improve their spelling and word recognition skills.\r\n\r\nFrom the award winning educational game developer.\r\n\r\nKids Spelling Fun has:\r\n• a large variety of over 500 English words to learn\r\n• high quality images set against colourful scenes that look great on High Definition (HD) and retina displays\r\n• spoken pronunciation for every word\r\n• the ability to learn using either uppercase or lowercase letter tiles \r\n• self paced learning in three distinct modes: learning, practise and test modes\r\n• increasing difficulty starting with easy three letter words and working up to eight letter words\r\n• additional word sets that cover specific topics such as animals, colors, fruit, numbers, shapes, transport and vegetables \r\n• no advertising\r\n\r\nKids Spelling Fun comes with a selection of free words to learn which can be easily upgraded through a single low cost in-app purchase to enable all 500+ words. Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it.
